The nose behind this fragrance is Aurélien Guichard. Top notes are Mint, Green Apple and Lemon; middle notes are Tonka Bean, Ambroxan and Geranium; base notes are Madagascar Vanilla, Virginian Cedar, Atlas Cedar, Vetiver and Oakmoss. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Versace is launching a new fragrance for men – Eros inspired by and deeply connected with Greek mythology. The aim of this edition is to reveal and release unrestrained passion and to accentuate desire. The fragrance was named after Greek god of love and son of goddess Aphrodite – Eros. Inspiration by ancient Greece has lasted since the time when Gianni Versace raised his fashion empire and took goddess Medusa as symbol of the brand to adorn numerous products of the house, among them also the new flacon of men's fragrance Eros.</p>

<p>The new perfume Eros is the first in the past five years to be launched and aimed at men. Donatella Versace's desire was to fit the fragrance into the concept of the Versace brand and to depict style and significance of long-lasting design, quality and popularity. "Eros is truly the DNA of the house of Versace" - explains Donatella. "We have a Greek motive making us think about ancient Greece, antiquities and mythology, while turquoise color represents the Mediterranean. That is Versace!"</p>

<p>Eros was created by Aurelien Guichard of Givaudan and it was announced as fresh, woody and slightly oriental. The fragrance includes mint oil combined with green apple and Italian lemon. Warmth is provided by tonka mixed with Venezuelan ambroxan and geranium flowers giving a fougere twist to the fragrance this way.</p>

<p>Flacon of the new fragrance for men Eros is created of turquoise color glass with head of Medusa on the body of the bottle and on its top. The fragrance is available as 50 and 100 ml EDT, along with accompanying perfumed body care products. Face of the advertising campaign is Brian Shimansky, while photographers are Mert &amp; Marcus. Donatella wanted a man-gladiator for the new campaign, who is fighting for what he wants, fighting for his goals. "This is a fragrance for a man who is his own master. He is a hero: a man who defends their ideas and goals." - stated Donatella Versace.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2319575" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EauDeSparta"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2290486.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EauDeSparta" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2319575ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2319575" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486">EauDeSparta</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 05:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Versace Eros EDT grabs my attention with its fresh opening. The top notes of bergamot, lemon, and mint give an energetic first impression. Then, the sweet heart notes come into play, creating a warm sensation with vanilla and tonka bean. Its longevity is quite impressive; it stays fresh throughout the day but i am not sure with new batches. The elegant packaging adds a luxurious touch to the fragrance. it has one of the coolest bottle designs. You'd buy it just for the empty bottle alone. It’s suitable for both day and night wear, but some might find the sweetness a bit overwhelming on hot summer days. Since it’s popular, I can sense that many people are using it. Still, it’s an appealing choice for me, and I often receive compliments, which makes wearing it even more enjoyable.<br />
<br />
Versace Eros EDT, ferah bir başlangıçla dikkatimi çekiyor. Bergamot, limon ve nane gibi üst notalar, ilk başta enerjik bir izlenim veriyor. Sonra tatlı kalp notalarının devreye girmesiyle; vanilya ve tonka fasulyesiyle sıcak bir his yaratıyor. Kalıcılığı da oldukça iyi; gün boyu üzerinizde kalıyor ancak yeni formülasyonlar sonucu kalıcılığını test etmedim. Şık ambalajı ise parfüme lüks bir hava katıyor.En havalı şişe tasarımına sahip parfümlerden birisi diyebilirim. Sadece boş şişesi bile alınır o derece. Gündüz ve gece kullanıma uygun ama tatlılığı gündüz kullanımında ve sıcak havalarda bazılarına fazla gelebilir. Popüler olduğu için herkesin kullandığını hissediyorum ancak çevremden de sıkça iltifat alıyor olmam kullanmayı keyifli hale getiriyor.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2316352" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DivineShrimp"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2287639"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2287639.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DivineShrimp" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2316352ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2316352" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2287639">DivineShrimp</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-15">10/15/24 07:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a good, inoffensive, citrusy fresh fragrance. You aren't going to wow somebody with this one, but you may get a few compliments.  I have the eau de toilette, so that's what I'm reviewing.<br />
<br />
It opens a little harsh with an alcohol smell that is very loud, but it disappears after about 5 minutes. When the alcohol disappears, you can really smell the lemon. you get hints of lemon and mint, and that's about it. I can't smell the apple or cedar at all, even after the dry-down.<br />
<br />
This is not a very complex fragrance, which can be a good thing. This is an easy to pickup and wear fragrance that almost anyone can pull off. Be careful with over spraying though, as the more synthetic-smelling notes will really shine and give people headaches.<br />
<br />
This is not something you'd wear to a formal event. Wear this when you're outside, at the gym, at school, ect.<br />
Overall I give this an 8/10. It's easy to wear, smells nice, and is very good for the price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2316352"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2316352#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2316034" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Anyway, not worth the price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2315452"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2315452#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2312751" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2307171" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Nick-Euphonia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2271678"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2271678.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Nick-Euphonia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2307171ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2307171" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2271678">Nick-Euphonia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-06">10/06/24 16:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tested from a carded sample.<br />
<br />
Opening is pure apple pie to me. The apple, tonka and vanilla notes combine to make this happen and my mind just goes straight to warm apple pie. I get the cedar and ambroxan later on, but it seems fairly linear over all. Very mass-appealing scent. I personally know people who had this (and Eros Flame) as their first fragrances and it's a perfect one for that. Perfect first fragrance. Easy to wear, versatile, reasonably priced, sweet, pleasing. Projects well, but I find that it doesn't have great longevity from what I've tested and worn of it (closer to 3 hour mark for me). I don't find it very unique, groundbreaking, or rich/complex. Personally, it doesn't resonate with me, and it's not something I'd be eager to wear again. It's extremely solid though. Scent is a 7.5/10. Over all is 7.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2307171"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2307171#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305425" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2305425" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="uoseph"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2276037"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2276037.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="uoseph" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2305425ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2305425" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2276037">uoseph</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-05">10/05/24 01:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A versatile fragrance for all occasions.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2305425"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2305425#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2303032" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2303032" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Carlitos"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1071323.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Carlitos" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Elixir-68415.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68415.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Elixir"title="Sauvage Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2303032ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2303032" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1071323">Carlitos</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-02">10/02/24 19:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>EROS, THE ANCIENT GREEK GOD OF LOVE<br />
<br />
Quote: "Women like it a lot. It's a real panty dropper!"<br />
This is an overstated opinion about Versace Eros, done by the probable biggest "YouTuber" influencer for men's fragrances.<br />
Judging by all the praise it received either from YouTube or from Blog reviewers, this fragrance seems to have it all. It is considered a "not to miss fragrance by any man". But is it really any good or any sexy?<br />
Well, both my wife and my daughter don't like it. I did like it, but my love for it ended some time ago. It's a nice fragrance but experience some fatigue with this type of fresh sweetness.<br />
I think Eros is a good clubbing fragrance. I also think that it's not the best choice for romantic dates or intimacy.<br />
It opens fresh (apple and citrus) and minty, preparing the way for an omnipresent tonka tamed by ambroxan, and offers you a very long vanilla accord with woody facets in the dry down.<br />
Without being similar, it follows the steps of Sauvage and Dylan Blue, but with added sweetness. It's a good mild/hot temperature perfume. It's particularly fitted for clubs, but also quite wearable on the beach where the choice is not broad. It's also particularly eclectic by being wearable during Spring and Autumn besides being a natural choice for the Summer. Just avoid using it in any cold weather type.<br />
I use it from time to time. Occasions may be a sunny Spring or Autumn day. It has also been stated that Eros is a "compliment magnet" or a "compliment gatherer". Well, that's not really my experience. People seem to like it or enjoy its sillage but don't go mad about it. "Spicebomb" or "Man in Black" attract more compliments without pulling off any person's underwear.<br />
Performance is above average for this type of pyramid, and the scent is never cloying or intrusive.<br />
The flask presentation is nice and stands out near other flasks in my collection.<br />
It's not a strictly unique fragrance. Various other fragrances have the same vibe type or reveal a fresh sweet scent like Eros does.<br />
I end up having a wide amount of places or situations where I can use it. It is proper for clubbing, office, by yourself, outdoor activities, work out, non formal people gatherings, informal meals,... and so on.<br />
<br />
My rates for Versace Eros:<br />
___ ___ ___ ___ ___<br />
- Scent Opening: 8.0<br />
- Scent Drydown: 8.0<br />
- Longevity: 8.0<br />
- Sillage: 8.0<br />
- Uniqueness: 8.5<br />
- Wearability: 8.5<br />
- Versatility: 9.0<br />
- Quality: 9.0<br />
- Presentation: 8.5<br />
- Price: 8.0 (this rating refers my judgment about its price when I bought it some years ago. I understand that the price rose since then, probably due to the "hype" raised by the NET reviewers. I don't know its actual average price, but I imagine that this rating should have a smaller value if I had bought Versace Eros today.)<br />
___ ___ ___ ___ ___<br />
- Overall rating: 8,35/10.00<br />
I received some questions about the EROS performance... Here is my experience:<br />
- Batch EM1710<br />
sillage - 4~6 feet (above average for this notes)<br />
projection - quite nice during the first 2~3 hours. It becomes a skin scent after 5~6 hours (above average for this notes)<br />
longevity - 7~8 hours (above average for this notes)<br />
Please note that performance is influenced by the production batch but also by the storage conditions before and after sale. If you store it with temperatures above 40º~45º centigrade or under direct sunlight for a month or so, the scent degrades and performance is cut in nearly half. yes... you must store it the same way you store red wine.<br />
I like this fragrance, but I am not sure if I will buy it again. I think I am going to switch it to Carven L`Eau Intense. I prefer Carven's less sweet scent (although preety similar) and it has a better performance.<br />
<br />
MUSIC: Marilyn Monroe - "I Wanna Be Loved By You"<br />
(Soundtrack of "Some Like It Hot")</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2303032"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2303032#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2302571" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I mean it smells as if you rubbed bazooka bubble gum on your wrist. But if that is your vibe, go for it. For those who have put this in the same family of CAHSEE are crazyyyyy. <br />
<br />
I would say this would be nice for 15-21 year olds who want that candy-smelling like cologne that is popular amongst the youngens. Outside that range, go for something with a little more elegance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2301710"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2301710#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2300296" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2211179">smellsgoodman66</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-24">09/24/24 19:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got this by accident after I ordered the clone from Maison Alhambra, so shout out to whomever made the mistake, I'm super appreciative. I'll be honest, it's not as sweet as I was expecting it to be, even in the dry down. The opening packs a punch; very citrusy and fresh apple fills the air, super pleasant. The dry down turns very green, like lemon grass and almost like fresh hay (in a good way); the vanilla is slight at best, the apple continues on somewhat understated but still noticeable, and it gets sweeter as it dries down. I don't really agree that this is just for young guys, I think you could wear this at any age. Will probably come back to edit when I've really gotten to try this out.<br />
<br />
edit: Coworker said that the hallway smelled like a sephora (in a good way.) He's notorious for being very picky with smells and he stated this one he really enjoyed and was thinking about getting it himself. So far everyone I've let try the fragrance has enjoyed how nice this is; so many compliments. The edt honestly is really good for the office as it's not super loud after 20 minutes or so but smells really fun and clean. Longevity is decent, it's around hour four atp and there's a nice little scent bubble around me that I quite enjoy. It can be a bit of a beast at first, a couple sprays into the air and you can smell it down the hall from my office, but it calms down really nicely. Honestly just an amazing, I'm very in love with this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2294124"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2294124#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294106" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1954658">isa12345678910</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-14">09/14/24 16:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>initial spray smells like any other male fragrance (in my opinion), but as it dries down you can start to smell the sweetness and the softness of the vanilla and cedar combo. for that reason, I’d argue that this fragrance leans more unisex than purely male. <br />
very simple perfume and it honestly  doesn’t stand out much (which can also be a good thing, if that’s something you prefer). it’s a well designed perfume - the notes pair very well, in my opinion. overall, I’d say that it’s a pretty safe choice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; ✅ Sweet and fresh fragrance that is mass appealing;<br />
✅ Perfect for a party or clubbing;<br />
✅ No matter how much hate it gets, if you wear this, most people will enjoy your smell, specially women. Don't be surprised if women prefer this scent over most 300$ niche fragrances.<br />
<br />
<br />
Cons:<br />
❌ The opening sweetness can be a bit headache inducing;<br />
❌ The longevity is much weaker with the reformulation. I definetly prefer the old batches;<br />
❌ Even though is still a great scent, it is a bit outdated now. I lean more the EDP, Parfum, flame or Born in Roma Coral fantasy more.<br />
<br />
Overall Score: 7,5<br />
Great scent, but i prefer other options today, mostly because of the newer batches. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2273341" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="elijah.rb71"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2238515"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2238515.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="elijah.rb71" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2273341ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2273341" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2238515">elijah.rb71</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-06">09/06/24 02:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yikes, it's been years since I owned a bottle of this, and I still can't figure out why I purchased it in the first place. This scent even drove me away from wanting to wear fragrance for a long time (Thanks D&amp;G Light Blue for bringing me back!) It's a very spicy fragrance to my nose, with lots of vanilla notes and some citrus thrown in. The result is a scent that smells like a very stuck-up douchey fraternity guy who is trying way too hard to be something that he's not. It could possibly be my overall dislike for straight up masculine scents, but I just can't get behind this one.<br />
<br />
Performance was never super fantastic for me. It lasted for a couple hours before the notes got muddled and even ickier than they were at the start, though the sillage was always pretty good! For those who may be curious, this is a pretty universal scent that can be worn pretty easily at any time of the year, and at any time of day as well. As I mentioned above, this is a very masculine scent, though I suppose with proper layering it may work in other ways as well. Overall, I can't say I care for this one much. Probably not the worst thing I've ever smelled, but certainly not wanting to smell it again anytime soon.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2273341"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2273341#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272055" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Wtf is that.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2262798"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2262798#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2259194" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2259194" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jetpack"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2230006"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2230006.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jetpack" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2259194ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2259194" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2230006">Jetpack</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 03:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Eros by Versace, launched in 2012 by Aurelien Guichard, is a fragrance that knows exactly what it’s doing. Named after the Greek god of love, this scent is all about passion and power, perfectly embodying the bold, flashy DNA of the Versace brand. Forget subtlety—Eros is designed to be a showstopper. It’s not here to offer niche sophistication; it’s here to grab attention and keep it.<br />
<br />
The scent starts with a bold mix of mint, lemon zest, and green apple—very vibrant and energetic. As it settles, I notice the warmth of tonka bean and ambroxan, creating a sweet and seductive vibe. The base notes of vanilla, vetiver, oakmoss, and cedarwood give it a lasting, magnetic finish.<br />
<br />
Critics may say it’s too obvious or too sweet, but that’s exactly the point. Eros isn’t trying to be niche or understated; it’s here to be a top contender in the luxury fragrance game. <br />
<br />
For a similar vibe, try its sibling scent, This is Him by Zadig &amp; Voltaire, also by Guichard, for another take on straightforward allure.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; This fragrance is more versatile than people claim it to be, i think it can be worn any season and any reason. This is not just a “clubbing scent”, this can be worn in school, work, date, almost anything. The performance is very good, projects a lot but longevity isn’t the best. I still prefer other Eros in the line, this EDT isn’t outdated but it can be outshined pretty easily. <br />
<br />
Scent: 8/10<br />
Versatility: 8/10<br />
Price: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 7/10<br />
<br />
Overall: 8.25/10, a solid fragrance that i recommend especially for a younger gentleman. The older gentleman should go for the higher concentrated ones like EDP and Parfum version.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2242101"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2242101#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2241000" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2202649">Mr_Mitch_Sorrenstein</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-23">07/23/24 23:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>God, I wanted to love this.<br />
<br />
It smelled great on the testers and it smelled great on my friend. But my skin just doesn’t take Eros well. Eros is supposed to be a sweet, minty, vanilla scent that immediately ‘drops panties’ (side note but can we as a community stop saying this dumbass phrase lmfao), but on my skin, it just smells incredibly bitter and nauseating. It isn’t that sweet to be honest, and I BARELY get any mint on mine. I sprayed a few times on a few occasions and it just simply doesn’t work on my body. Performance is moderate, maybe 5-8 hours on me. Sillage is also good.<br />
<br />
Eros’s brother, Eros Flame, is absolutely stellar, though. That spice mixed with the vanilla and citrus drives me insane! I highly recommend Eros Flame over the original Eros; I think it’s way more interesting as a fragrance and has a bit of an edgier vibe to it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2221144" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MYAtomizer;)"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2150833"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2150833.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MYAtomizer;)" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Roja-Dove/Elysium-Pour-Homme-Parfum-Cologne-46296.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.46296.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Elysium Pour Homme Parfum Cologne"title="Elysium Pour Homme Parfum Cologne"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2221144ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2221144" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2150833">MYAtomizer;)</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-17">07/17/24 06:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Part 2<br />
Now that my Eros finally has arrived in mail and smelled it. I want to clarify for you what the difference is between the formula from the newer versions and the OG formula from 2012 wich i have in my hand at the moment of this writing.<br />
<br />
We all know that the formula has changed in eros, that is, not necessarily worse, but lighter in terms of the scent. The factor with the new formula is that the scent is not long-lasting, it doesn't last long at all. I would say between 2-3 hours, then the scent becomes more like a skin scent.<br />
<br />
While the formula that I have here in my hand, which I call the gold liquid, lasts a very long time, I would say between 5-8 hours, if not the whole day as well and I am not exaggerating at all. But it is not only about how long-lasting the fragrance is in the 2012 formula, but also that it spreads very well compared to the newer versions of eros.<br />
<br />
The bottom line is that, yes, it is verified by me that the formula has changed over the years for eros, and that the OG formula in eros is the strongest of all the recent eros. However, I would never forget to point out that only 1 if not 2 sprays are enough for the 2012 formula due to how strong and vibrant it is. While the newer ones may require up to 5-7 sprays to feel it later in the day.<br />
<br />
Hope this helped with the difference between the OG formula (2012), and the newer formulas for eros (2017-2022)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2221144"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2221144#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2221000" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Smell: 7/10<br />
Performance : 7/10<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2069156">Mazov</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-16">06/16/24 12:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This isn't really a scent I'd normally go for as I tend to like more classic aromatic fougeres, but I got this as a gift. <br />
<br />
It's OK. Well blended, sweet, youthful, mass-appealing. I mainly get minty vanilla with a bit of citrus with a woodsy dry down. It's very easy to wear and casual, 'breezy' comes to mind as an adjective. My girlfriend really likes it. <br />
<br />
Longevity and sillage seem very weak to me, it feels as though it's a skin scent within 1 hour and totally gone within 3 hours although I'm fairly certain that's just my nose being sensitive to ambroxan. That's the throughline in the DNA tying this to Dylan Blue to me. <br />
<br />
Wouldn't have picked this up personally but grateful for the gift, will probably end up wearing this occasionally, especially since it's a crowd-pleaser. If you're the type who only wants a handful of 'the hits' when it comes to fragrances, this seems like a must-have. Personally I don't find there to be anything too special about it, but it's far from bad.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2190143"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2190143#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2189843" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I also would not buy this under any circumstance, especially for its price of 70£/100ml.<br />
<br />

Sillage - 4/10<br />
Longevity - 6/10<br />
Bottle - 8/10<br />
Popularity - Overrated</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2184000"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2184000#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2183955" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2162062" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tracershy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1181886"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="tracershy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Azzaro/The-Most-Wanted-66826.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.66826.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="The Most Wanted"title="The Most Wanted"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2162062ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2162062" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1181886">tracershy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-20">05/20/24 09:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A fresh and sweet fragrance for young boys.  He has a carefreeness that suits a 20-year-old more than an older guy.<br />
 The beginning is a fresh mix of expressive mint, sweet apple and tart lemon juice.  After a short while, only lemon tartness remains from this mix.  Quite quickly, a slightly nauseating tonka appears, followed by a sweet, quite sticky, artificial vanilla.  Over time there are more woody and mossy notes.  After about an hour, we already have a lot of tonka-vanilla sweetness mixed with ambroxan, which keeps the composition in a masculine tone.  For me, this ambroxan is too harsh and irritating.<br />
 Eros is quite universal, it suits different seasons and different occasions, but rather very casual, because there is a lot of youthful ease and simplicity in this fragrance and therefore it lacks any depth.<br />
 Due to a lot of sweetness, it is not suitable for summer, in the heat it is bland and suffocating.<br />
 The parameters are the same, longevity is about 5 hours, projection is rather low.<br />
 Overall it's not a bad scent but definitely not for me, it's too flat and bland.  Not to my taste, but I'm a bit older than my 20s.  You may like it, especially young people.<br />
<br />
6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2162062"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2162062#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2161763" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2155494" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jonathan.penman"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2094438"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2094438.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jonathan.penman" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2155494ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2155494" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2094438">jonathan.penman</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-14">05/14/24 06:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Good fragrance, but not to my taste.<br />
<br />
I like the sweetness of the vanilla note, but it feels a bit too bright with not enough warmth.<br />
<br />
I can see why girls might like this smell, whether they want it on guys, or want to wear it themselves, but to me it lacks mystery or sexiness.<br />
<br />
Performance is not terrible, but I have definitely seen better. On my arms it only lasts around six hours, but on my neck it can still be smelt up to around twelve hours. On my clothes it can last for days.<br />
<br />
I would say this is more of a night-time fragrance, but can be worn in the day too. Good for every season, though I can't really imagine it being worn in Autumn too well, as it is too bright and sweet for that.<br />
<br />
This fragrance reminds me of a young teenager dressed up for an evening occasion, not too formal, but certainly smarter or better dressed than a casual party. I just find the fragrance to be a bit too childish, which I have heard is a theme across most of the newer Versace fragrances. If that suits your personality—youthful, bright, playful, possibly a bit naïve, but also a bit romantic—then I would say this is for you. Otherwise I would not necessarily recommend.<br />
<br />
Nevertheless, it still seems to be quite a mass-appealing fragrance and even if you don't like it, it will still garner compliments.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; This can be worn all year long besides winter. I don't believe this would unfold &amp; perform well in cold weather in my humble opinion. Eros is definitely an attention grabber, a crowd pleaser, &amp; a panty dropper. Even if you don't receive any compliments. Believe me when I say this "Women will stand more closer to you than usual &amp; look in your direction a little more. This is a masculine fragrance without any of the "Gentleman Aura" or the "Macho man" vibes touch to it. Probably because "Versace" fragrances &amp; their clothing are more marketed towards homosexual males. But heterosexual men can still wear this stuff as well. <br />
<br />
The longevity is good. But I still layer my cologne with essential oils that are inspired by the fragrance itself to get the performance &amp; scent trail that I truly desire without having to keep overspraying myself. <br />
<br />
This is great for.<br />
<br />
1)Spring, Summer, &amp; Fall. <br />
2)Job/Office. <br />
3)Happy Hour.<br />
4)Clubbing/Partying atmosphere. <br />
5)Hanging with women. <br />
6)Dressing down or casual. <br />
7)Trying to be noticed. <br />
8)Going on a date. <br />
9)Evenings/Nights.<br />
10)Damped rainy days. <br />
<br />
I wouldn't necessarily reach for this. <br />
<br />
1)Winter. <br />
2)Hanging with the fellas. <br />
3)Dressing sophisticated. <br />
4)Attending a formal event. <br />
5)Gym.<br />
6)Outdoor activities. <br />
7)Very hot outside (Warm days are more appropriate for this fragrance)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2151472"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2151472#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2151209" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's a likeable everyday scent. I tried both EDP and EDT and I must say that I liked EDT more because EDP smells "older". All in all this is a Masculine Clubbing fragrance that will give you a younger aura.<br />
<br />
I'd say that this is a best of both worlds, it has a minty sweet green apple opening like you just came out the shower and the drydown is a intimate ambroxan vanilla. Only few of the "fresh" fragrance that can pull off the sweet Vanilla with it. I'm in love with the gourmand drydown, this is an absolute banger for people who love vanilla like me. It's almost like it's made for you to go to the club smelling fresh and smell like a sweet snack after you got a woman on your bed.<br />
<br />
I tried both Eros and Eros Flame at Sephora and preferred this over the "flanker" Eros Flame. Opening was too spicy and citrusy that if you have body odor when you sweat, you'll smell like a stink bomb. Almost every tester in Sephora stores smell nothing like the original though.<br />
<br />
Cheap and a reliable must have in your collection.<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2146520"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2146520#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2146496" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I was a little hesitant when aquiring Eros EDT. The price was good, just under £50 for 100ml. I have to say this is a great fragrance. Full marks for versatility. It’s suitable for all seasons in my opinion. Yes it’s a simple fragrance but it’s a beauty. Fresh mint at the top with a mildly sweet base. Not overly sweet as I thought it might be. Also not particularly youthful. I am middle aged man and really enjoy the wearing experience. I just know I am smelling fresh clean and approachable. I have lots of fragrances. Some much more expensive. This often criticised scent is bizarrely becoming one of my favourites. If you are a fan of the Armani Code line. Although they smell nothing alike they do similar a job.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2136340"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2136340#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2135153" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1673973">ethan-fragrantica</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-20">04/20/24 11:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Eros by Versace: <br />
What a fragrance. This was my first proper frag and got me into the world of fragrances and I genuinely think it's one of the best (I'm very biased ahaha). It sometimes gets a bad rep and yes it's overworn but it's popular for a reason. It's incredibly versatile-any time, any place, any season. You can wear it to the club or just to chill and with the flankers it works for any age. Amazing performance and amazing longevity. It's aromatic, green and fresh with a nice vanillic and woody base. You don't necessarily have to love it but you do have to try it. I doubt it will be going out of fashion anytime soon and it's worth the price point. <br />
<br />
Top notes: Lemon, mint, apple<br />
Middle notes: Tonka, ambroxan, slight geranium<br />
Base notes: Really smooth mix of dusty vanilla and cedar<br />
<br />
Longevity: 4.5/5<br />
Sillage: 4.5/5<br />
Scent: 5/5<br />
Design: 5/5<br />
Gender: Masculine<br />
Overall: 5/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="2130641"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=2130641#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2130039" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1014646">TonyAKAMrClean</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-09-28">09/28/16 18:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm with you positive folks...<br />
<br />
Yes, it's not a Dior or a niche. Big whoop! I've avoided reviewing this one because of the review bashing going on, but for me, this is a great loud scent for hanging out with the guys. I don't wear it for the women, I wear it for myself. I wear it when I'm confident, and maybe a little cocky. I wear it when I have absolutely zero desire to impress anyone and when I don't really care what anyone thinks. I have however received quite a few compliments on it. <br />
<br />
To me, it smells better than Le Male, as that was its competition when I bought it. I couldn't stand Le Male, but I love the note separation in Eros. The vanilla and mint are very distinct and separate, yet very well balanced by the tonka. It starts out smooth and LOUD! Then it dries down spicy and intimate while retaining good projection until it's gone. Luckily, my skin eats the vanilla-mint alive, so I tend to get more of the scent of the drydown for the duration of the fragrance, but on others' skin, it tends to remain more minty. <br />
<br />
Most days, I'll pick up Eros and give it a sniff, and it doesn't match my mood. But on the days that it does, it's the only scent that fits. Nothing else in my collection fits that mood, and although I don't wear Eros often, it has earned a home within my collection. <br />
<br />
Bottom line: Don't feel ashamed for your fragrance tastes. Cheap, expensive, doesn't matter. Wear what you like. That's the POINT of fragrances! Some of the best scents in my collection are also the cheapest, and some of my favorites are among the most "synthetic".<br />
<br />
For the love of fragrance, happy sniffing.  ;-)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="747181"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=747181#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent419793" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It can also work for the mature man (30+) who is both confident and willing to wear an attractive, creamy, soft-sweet fragrance for men, worn in moderation.  I have found this fragrance to be such a smooth, soothing, and incredibly "self-satisfying" everyday/casual scent when  appropriately applied (as other similarly-stated reviews here "convinced" me a year ago). I quite enjoy the scent of Eros, but I am equally grateful for how it makes me FEEL (ie. calm, relaxed, content, with a sense of "life is good" throughout my day).  It is actually this latter quality that makes it doubly hard NOT to reach for Eros-- Essentially I am now a 50-plus year old addict of this fragrance! <br />
<br />
So if you are 30+ and interested, definitely try before you buy with a "light to normal" wearing of Eros--waiting at least an hour into the dry-down to allow the minty open to fully settle-in, getting creamy smooth..... with the vanilla, tonka, apple, lemon, and woods. Don't over-apply lest you find it too sweet, cloying or having a clubbing effect.  You may just be VERY pleasantly surprised with what you discover!  I find Eros is best worn in the Fall, Winter, and most Spring days. I have a mid-2017 batch having near-perfect light to moderate projection with beastly longevity @ 17 hours on skin and a solid 7+ days on clothes! (no exaggeration....)   8.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="1024874"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=1024874#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent874554" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; #6 Versace Eros, project 2hrs, last 6hrs<br />
<br />
I ♥ EROS but for an entirely different set of reasons:<br />
• EROS is loud enough for clubbing, but also<br />
• EROS is also Calm (relaxing) enough for working<br />
• EROS is romatic for dating, and <br />
• EROS is relaxing enough for aromatic therapy<br />
• EROS MINT give it a Summer Freshness<br />
• EROS VANILLA give it Strength to in Fall &amp; Winter<br />
• EROS = 10/10 in all season VERSATILITY<br />
<br />
EROS has no Weakness, other than a poorly conceive<br />
marketing as a Club scent.  People jump on the HATE<br />
Train without discovering its Theraputic qualities.<br />
<br />
EROS is actually better on【Older Mature People】<br />
Its soothing, calming, qualities give it a vibe of a <br />
Mature Confident Man (who doesn't need to prove).<br />
<br />
Younger Men might be better off with Paco Rabanne<br />
Invectus / 1 Million / Black XS, PB Frag have serious<br />
ATTITUDE that makes you STAND OUT in clubs.<br />
<br />
Lastly, don't jump on the HYPE or HATE trains, judge<br />
each Fragrance with your own nose, the results may<br />
surprise you.  I was expecting an Attitude Loud Frag,<br />
but what I get is a Calm Soothing Romantic scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="874554"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=874554#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent353208" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/297374">Kostas_Minimal</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2013-04-05">04/05/13 11:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tried this today and i really dont understand the hate on this one.Its not something revolutionary or new but its damn good to my nose.<br />
It starts like a very sweet sticky lemonade (really unique opening) and it drys to a sweet kinda spicy thick vanilla,which is nothing new but it ISNT bad.It kinda reminds me something like between axe and rochas...<br />
Projection is above average so is longetivity....<br />
Its a very sensual fragrance and its great for a summery evening in a greek island.I can clearly understand the concept versace had with this one but dont know why people dont like eros.The bottle also is a piece of art.STUNNING.Among the best ive seen...<br />
<br />
Overall score: 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="353208"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=353208#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="16657" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/754409">Anosmic</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-06-09">06/09/14 19:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a great attention grabber.  You can smell a ton of colognes at the store and smell this toward the end and despite nose fatigue, this still will stand out.  Great projection and longevity as well.  <br />
<br />
As a club scent I can see this being great.  If it can stand out and smell decent after smelling 20 other colognes in a store, then I imagine at a club where it is competing with the One Millions and Le Males, etc., it will do the same.  <br />
<br />
The difficulty I have with this scent is that it just doesn't feel well put together if I haven't smelled 20 other colognes first and am suffering from nose fatigue.  It is as if the vanilla, citrus and mint are not blended correctly or just don't work well together here.   I do not personally enjoy the scent. <br />
<br />
But, hey, others do enjoy it and it will definitely catch people's attention even when surrounded by competing scents.  Apparently that is what it was designed to do,... and it does it well.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16657"comment_id="494080"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-16657.html?ccid=494080#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent587839" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; And that alone should make me wanna wear it, right? No. <br />
<br />
I just straight up don't like this one. It's way too strong, too potent, sickly sweet, the mint is awful. It gives me an headache. (Yes, just pop those ballons lol)<br />
<br />
And i've reached a point in my fragrance journey, where I really don't care about compliments anymore. I only wear fragrances I truly like, and feel fantastic wearing, to boost my own confidence. And that shows. I'm done with wearing fragrances I don't really like, loud fragrances that fills the room, to get reactions from my surroundings. I'm feeling great, being in my own little scent 'bubble', where people only smells me when I invite them in to my intimate 'bubble'.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;
